*Main category:* **[English prefixes](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Category:English_prefixes "Category:English prefixes")**

English has many [prefixes](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/prefixes "prefixes") that are used to construct words, particularly in scientific and medical language. For a list of suffixes, see [Appendix:English suffixes](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:English_suffixes "Appendix:English suffixes").

This page organizes prefixes alphabetically. To see this content sorted by category, see [Appendix:English prefixes by semantic category](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:English_prefixes_by_semantic_category "Appendix:English prefixes by semantic category"). For a list of prefixes specifically for nationalities, ethnic groups, and languages see [Appendix:English nationality prefixes](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:English_nationality_prefixes "Appendix:English nationality prefixes"). For SI prefixes: [Appendix:SI units](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:SI_units "Appendix:SI units").

## A

| Prefix | All forms | Definition | Example | Category | Subcat | Subsub | Crosscat | Alt-Sort |

| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_up "a-") <sup>01</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_up "a-") <sup>01</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) Forming verbs with the sense *away*, *up*, *on*, *out*. | e.g. [arise](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/arise "arise"), [await](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/await "await") | Abstract | Spatial |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_asthough "a-") <sup>02</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_asthough "a-") <sup>02</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) Forming verbs with the sense of intensified action. | e.g. *[abide](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/abide#English "abide")*, *[amaze](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/amaze#English "amaze")* | Abstract | Similarity |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_having "a-") <sup>03</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_having "a-") <sup>03</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) [In](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/in "in"), [on](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/on "on"), [at](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/at "at"); used to show a state, condition, or manner. Also passing into sense 2. | e.g. [apace](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/apace "apace"), [afire](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/afire "afire"), [aboil](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/aboil "aboil"), [a-bling](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-bling "a-bling") | Abstract | Possession |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_into "a-") <sup>04</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_into "a-") <sup>04</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) In, into. |  | Abstract | Spatial |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_toward "a-") <sup>05</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_toward "a-") <sup>05</sup> | In the direction of, or [toward](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/toward "toward"). | e.g. [astern](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/astern "astern"), [abeam](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/abeam "abeam") | Abstract | Spatial |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_this "a-") <sup>06</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_this "a-") <sup>06</sup> | ([archaic](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic "Appendix:Glossary"), [dialectal](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal "Appendix:Glossary")) At such a time. |  | Abstract | Specificity |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_doing "a-") <sup>07</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_doing "a-") <sup>07</sup> | ([archaic](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic "Appendix:Glossary"), [dialectal](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal "Appendix:Glossary")) In the act or process of. Used in some dialects before a present participle. |  | Abstract | Completion |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_participle "a-") <sup>08</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_participle "a-") <sup>08</sup> | General indicator of a participle, often a past particple. | e.g. [aware](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/aware "aware"), [alike](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/alike "alike") | Abstract | Temporal |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_pastparticiple "a-") <sup>09</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_pastparticiple "a-") <sup>09</sup> | ([Devon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Country_English "w:West Country English")) Used to form the past participle of a verb. | e.g. [a-gone](https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=a-gone&action=edit&redlink=1 "a-gone (page does not exist)"), [a-seen](https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=a-seen&action=edit&redlink=1 "a-seen (page does not exist)") | Abstract | Temporal |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_fully "a-") <sup>10</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_fully "a-") <sup>10</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) Forming words with the sense of wholly, or utterly out. | e.g. [abash](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/abash "abash") | Abstract | Completion |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_not "a-") <sup>11</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_not "a-") <sup>11</sup> | [Not](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/not "not"), without, opposite of. | e.g. [amoral](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/amoral "amoral"), [asymmetry](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/asymmetry "asymmetry"), [atheism](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/atheism "atheism"), [asexual](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/asexual "asexual"), [acyclic](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/acyclic "acyclic"), [atypical](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/atypical "atypical") | Abstract | Negation |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_towards "a-") <sup>12</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_towards "a-") <sup>12</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) Towards; Used to indicate direction, reduction to, increase to, change into, or motion. | e.g. [ascend](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/ascend "ascend"), [aspire](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/aspire "aspire"), [amass](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/amass "amass"), [abandon](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/abandon "abandon"), [avenue](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/avenue "avenue") | Abstract | Completion |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_away "a-") <sup>13</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_away "a-") <sup>13</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) Away from. | e.g. *[avert](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/avert#English "avert")*, *[aperient](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/aperient#English "aperient")*, *[abridge](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/abridge#English "abridge")*, *[assoil](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/assoil#English "assoil")* | Abstract | Spatial |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_of "a-") <sup>14</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_of "a-") <sup>14</sup> | (no longer [productive](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#productive "Appendix:Glossary")) Of, from. | e.g. [anew](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/anew "anew"), [afresh](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/afresh "afresh") | Abstract | Origin |  |  |  |
| **[a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_emptysyllable "a-") <sup>15</sup>** | [a-](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/a-#English:_emptysyllable "a-") <sup>15</sup> | Empty syllable added to songs, poetry, verse and other speech. | e.g. [**A-** tisket **a-** tasket](https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=%27%27%27A-%27%27%27tisket_%27%27%27a-%27%27%27tasket&action=edit&redlink=1 "'''A-'''tisket '''a-'''tasket (page does not exist)") | Colours, shapes, and textures | Sounds |  |  |  |

Here the surrounding time periods are indicated by the prefix and not the intervening event. | e.g. [interlocution](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/interlocution "interlocution"), [interact](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/interact "interact"), [intercycle](https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/intercycle "intercycle") | Abstract | Temporal |  |  |  |
